### System — 2026-07-01T21:03:18.816862

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Current State (Loop 1 audit)**  
- **Equity/Available:** 0.0 (stale) – caused by HTTP 429 rate‑limit on `/api/v1/account/balance`; fallback to disk snapshot may be outdated.  
- **Open Positions:** 2 shorts  
  1. BAS‑USDT ‑1 contract (avg 0.04027, unrealized ‑0.000505 USDT)  
  2. VELVET‑USDT ‑1 contract (avg 1.5412, unrealized +0.12111 USDT)  
- **Trade restrictions:** buys allowed; sells/short‑adds blocked for both symbols (blocked‑sell list).  
- **TP/SL:** missing on both positions (`positions_missing_tpsl`).  
- **Health:** degraded, confidence 0.78.  

**Key Issues**  
1. Equity/available margin unreadable → margin checks unreliable.  
2. 429 rate‑limit on balance endpoint → may block future balance fetches/orders.  
3. Live API returned empty data → possible connectivity/throttling.  
4. Open positions lack TP/SL → unmanaged risk.  

**Immediate Repair Recommendations (already identified)**  
- Implement exponential back‑off, retry balance fetch after ~120 s; cache balance data.  
- Verify/refresh `equity‑cache.json`; flag if stale.  
- Call `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` (or `blofin_place_tpsl`) for BAS‑USDT and VELVET‑USDT (e.g., TP +5 %, SL ‑5 %).  
- Log 429 incident, trigger self‑heal playbook entry “API rate‑limit handling”.  
- Skip additional short‑adds on blocked symbols this cycle; scan universe for alternative candidates.  

**User Request (21:02:49)**  
> Run a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack. Use `blofin_get_stack_health` and `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report`. Output strict JSON with fields: `status`, `issues`, `repair_actions`, `confidence`, `narrative`.  

**Available Tools (relevant)**  
- `blofin_get_stack_health` – returns operational health snapshot (caches, feeds, errors, equity).  
- `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` – returns latest swarm learning, improvements, self‑fixes.  

**Open Action**  
Execute the two functions as per user request and format the combined result into the required JSON structure.

**What this means for the swarm’s operation**

- **Visibility gap:** Users cannot see mesh‑fulfillment or clique‑rugged status on the dashboard, which defeats the “rugg​ed” resilience guarantee.
- **Partial mesh fulfillment:** Only 3 of 15 agents have completed their audit/crutch cycles; the remaining 12 agents must finish their peer‑audit checks before the mesh can be considered complete.
- **Pending pipeline steps:** The trading pipeline, oversight monitoring, and learning‑compound stages are still marked as pending for cycle 1, indicating that no trades have been fully executed or verified yet.
- **Self‑heal loop is active:** The swarm has already logged the corrective action and will auto‑apply it on the next recurrence, but until the UI markers and pending audits are fixed, the system remains in a degraded state.

**Recommended immediate repair actions (to be executed by the Ops‑Monitor Agent)**

1. **Refresh dashboard UI** – add the missing markers (`mesh_fulfillment`, `meshFulfillment`, `clique_rugged`, `cliqueRugged`) in `swarm_dashboard.html` and ensure the graph API returns them.
2. **Trigger a full mesh audit** – run `run_polymorphic_mesh_audit()` to re‑evaluate all 210 peer links; capture any weak links.
3. **Complete pending agent audits** – for each pending agent, invoke its peer‑audit routine (e.g., `Ops-Monitor-Agent` audits `Trading-Director`, etc.) until all 12 agents report status = `fulfilled`.
4. **Finalize task‑completion audit** – run `audit_cycle_tasks()` and automatically repair any phantom‑done entries; then clear the “oversight” non‑terminal flag.
5. **Verify pipeline progression** – after the above steps, confirm that `trading_pipeline` and `learning_compound` move to `completed` and that new orders appear in the trade journal with valid `orderId`s.
6. **Log the repair** – add entries to `self_heal_playbook` so future recurrences auto‑apply the same fixes without manual intervention.

Once these actions are performed, re‑run `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` to confirm the mesh fulfillment reaches **15 / 15** and the dashboard markers appear, restoring the swarm to a **healthy** (rich) state.  

---  

*End of analysis.*  



### End of Loop 1
